        $(document).ready(function () {

            // show thge logo on scroll
            $(document).bind('scroll', function () {
                if ($(this).scrollTop() > 225) {
                    $("#smalllogo").fadeIn('1000');
                    $("#profilebar").addClass("scrolled");
                } else {
                    $("#smalllogo").hide();
                    $("#profilebar").removeClass("scrolled");
                }
            });
            $("#searchinput").autocomplete({
                source: "autocomplete.php",
                minLength: 3,
                select: function (event, ui) {
                    var url = ui.item.id;
                    if (url != '#') {
                        location.href = '/' + url;
                    }
                },
                open: function (event, ui) {
                    $(".ui-autocomplete").css("z-index", 1000);
                }
            });


            $("#banner").click(
                function (e) {
                    if (e.target.id == "banner") {
                        window.location = 'https://www.crossresults.com';
                    }
                }
            );
            $("#searchinput").click(
                function () { return false; }
            );

            $("#searchform").submit(function () {
                return $("#searchinput").val() != "";
            });

        });

        if (!document.addEventListener) {
            //IE8 fix
            $(function () {
                //DOM has loaded, put your code here
                setupResponsiveNav();
            });
        }
        else {
            document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () { setupResponsiveNav(); })
        }


        function setupResponsiveNav() {
            $("#nav").show();

            /* call responsive nav */
            var navigation = responsiveNav("#nav", { // Selector: The ID of the wrapper
                animate: true, // Boolean: Use CSS3 transitions, true or false
                transition: 400, // Integer: Speed of the transition, in milliseconds
                label: "menu", // String: Label for the navigation toggle
                insert: "before", // String: Insert the toggle before or after the navigation
                customToggle: "", // Selector: Specify the ID of a custom toggle
                openPos: "relative", // String: Position of the opened nav, relative or static
                jsClass: "js", // String: 'JS enabled' class which is added to <html> el
                init: function () { }, // Function: Init callback
                open: function () { }, // Function: Open callback
                close: function () { } // Function: Close callback
            });
        }
        function UpdateUpgrades() {
            var cat = $("#category").val();
            var region = $("#region").val();

            $.cookie("upgradecategory", cat, { expires: 30 });
            $.cookie("upgraderegion", region, { expires: 30 });

            var ajaxMsg = "<div style=\"text-align:center;\"><img src=\"img/snake_transparent.gif\"/></div>";
            $("#upgradeboard").html(ajaxMsg);

            $("#upgradeboard").load("upgradeboard.php?cat=" + cat + "&region=" + region + "&sn=r");
        }

$(document).ready(function(){ 
	
    $(".getRacersButton").click(function() {
        var searchText = $("#searchText").val();
		if(searchText.length > 0)
		{
			var url = "ajaxracers.php?s="+escape(searchText) + "&team=yes&confirm=1";
			
			$(".target").html("<img src='img/snake_transparent.gif'/>");
			$(".target").load(url, function(response, status, xhr){			
				});
			$(".input").hide();
			$("#profilesearchresults").show();
		}
		else
		{
			alert('Type your name in the box first, guy');
			$("#searchText").val('THIS BOX!');
			$("#searchText").focus();
			$("#searchText").select();
		}
        });
	$(".togglelogin").click(function(){
		$("#loginform").modal({maxWidth: 600,overlayClose:true, maxHeight: 600 });
		$("#CreateAccountButton").click(function(){
            
            var email = $("#newemail").val();
            var pass = $("#newpass").val();
            var racerID = $("#racerID").val();
            var valid = true;
            var error = "";
            if(email.indexOf("@") == -1)
            {
                valid = false;
                error = "Invalid email.";
            }
            if(pass.length == 0)
            {
                valid = false;
                error = "No zero length passwords.";
            }
            if(valid)
            {
                          
				
                var data = { email: email, pass: pass, racerID:racerID };
                $("#CreateAccountTarget").html("<div style=\"text-align: center\">Creating Account...</div>");                
                $("#CreateAccountTarget").load("procNewAccount.php",data);
            }
            else
            {
                alert(error);
            }
            return false;
        });
		return false;
	});
	$("#SubmitButton").click(function(){
            //var pass = $("#newpass").val();
            //var hexpass = hex_md5(pass);  
            //$("#newpass").val(hexpass);
        });
    $("#regiononly").click(function(){
        var checked = ($("#regiononly").is(':checked'));
        window.location = "setprofile.php?setregionpref="+checked;
    });
    $("a.togglebutton").click(function(){
			
            $(this).next().toggle("slow");
            var expander = $(this).children().children("img");
            if(expander.attr("src") == "img/minus.png")
            {
                expander.attr("src","img/plus.png");
            }
            else
            {
                expander.attr("src","img/minus.png");
            }
            return false;
        });
	    
});

{
        var name = (jQueryObj.text());
         var id = jQueryObj.children(".racerID").val();
         window.location = "setprofile.php?id="+id;
		 
}

<script type="text/javascript" src="//www.gstatic.com/charts/loader.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    google.charts.load('current', { 'packages': ['corechart'] });
    google.charts.setOnLoadCallback(chartInitialize);
    function chartInitialize() {
        GraphDataService("/racerhistorygraph.php?racerID=15961&type=pct&subtype=pts&json=1",updateChart);
    }

      function GraphDataService(endpoint, onsuccess) {
                
                $.ajax({
                    type: "GET",
                    contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                    url: endpoint,
                    async: true,
                    dataType: "json",
                    success: function (data, status) {
                        if(status == "success") {
                            if (onsuccess != undefined) {
                                onsuccess(data._data);
                            }
                        } else {
                            $("#graphtarget").hide();
                        }
                    },
                    error: function(data,status){
                        $("#graphtarget").hide();
                    }
                });
            }
     function updateChart(data){
              
              var total = 0;
              var compareTotal = 0;
              if(data.length > 1){
                  var graphData = new Array();
                  var cols = data.length;
                  
                  graphData[0] = new Array();
                  graphData[0][0] = 'Race';
                  graphData[0][1] = 'Points';                  
          
                  var totalraces = data.length;
                  var min = 9999;
                  var max = 0;
                  for(i = 0; i < data.length; i++)
                  {
                      graphData[i+1] = new Array();                           
                                                   
                      graphData[i+1][0] = data[i].X
                      graphData[i+1][1] = data[i].Y;                   

                      if(data[i].Y < min)
                        min = data[i].Y;
                      if(data[i].Y > max)
                        max = data[i].Y;

                  }
                   
                  if(max <= 1){
                    max = 1;
                    min = 0;
                  } else { 
                    min = min-50;
                  }

                  var options = {
                     
                      fontSize: 16,
                      //fontName: '"Open Sans", "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, Arial, Geneva, sans-serif',
                      hAxis: { titleTextStyle: {color: '#333'}, minValue: 0},
                      vAxis: {minValue: min, maxValue: max,
                        viewWindow: { min: min, max: max}
                        },
                      legend: { position: "bottom" },
                      animation: {"startup": true,
                          duration: 1000,
                          easing: 'out'
                      }, 
                      chartArea: {
                          left: 40,
                          top: 20,
                          width: '95%'
                      },
                      series: {
                          0: { color: '#FC6719' },
                          1: { color: '#C4C4C4' }
                        }
                    };
                  $("#graphtarget").animate({height: "250px"}, 100,"swing",function(){
                        var chart = new google.visualization.AreaChart(document.getElementById('graphtarget'));
                        var dt = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable(graphData);
                        chart.draw(dt, options);
                  });
                }
            }

    $(document).ready(function(){ 
        $(".download").click(function(){ $(this).hide(); $(this).next().fadeToggle() });
		$(".MetaDataSubmit").click(function(){
			var url = $(this).prev().val();
			var error = false;
			if(url.trim() == "" || url.indexOf(".") == -1)
			{
				alert("You need to enter a url, dude.");
				error = true;
			}
			return !error;
		});
        $('.showupgradepoints').click(function(){
            $(".totalupgradepoints").toggle("fast");
                    return false;
        });
			$(".togglechallenge").click(function(){ 
			$(this).next().toggle(); 
			$(this).hide(); 
			$(this).prev().hide(); 
			$(this).next().next().hide(); 
			});
		$(".challengesubmit").click(function(){
			var data = $(this).parent().children(".challengeemail").val();
			var target = $(this).attr("targetID");
			var postthis = { email: data, targetid: target };
			if(data)
			{
				$(this).parent().children(".challengesubmittarget").html("Challenging...");
				$(this).parent().children(".challengesubmittarget").load("procNewChallenge.php",postthis);
			}
			else
			{
				alert('Enter an email, punk');
			}
		});
		
		$(".editteamsubmit").click(function(){
			var newTeamName = $(this).parent().children("input").val();
			
			var resultID = $(this).parent().children("input").attr("rID");
			 
			$(this).parent().hide();
			$(this).parent().next().show();
			
			$(this).parent().next().load("updateTeamName.php?rID="+resultID+"&team="+encodeURIComponent(newTeamName));
		});
		        $(".editteambutton").click(function(){
			$(this).parent().hide();
			$(this).parent().prev().show();
		});
        $("a.expandMonth").click(function(){
        
            $(this).next().toggle("slow");
            var expander = $(this).children().children("img");
            if(expander.attr("src") == "img/minus.png")
            {
                expander.attr("src","img/plus.png");
            }
            else
            {
                expander.attr("src","img/minus.png");
            }
            return false;
        });
		$("#head2headall").click(function(){
			
			$(".popup1").html("<Center><img src='img/snake_transparent.gif'></Center>");
			$(".popup1").load("headtoheadall.php?racerID="+15961, function(){ $(".popup1").modal({overlayClose:true}); });
		});
		$(".addmeta").click(function(event){
			
			var theDiv = $(this).next()

			//var tPosX = event.pageX;
			//var tPosY = event.pageY+10;
			//theDiv.css({top: tPosY, left: tPosX});
			theDiv.toggle();
			return false;
		});
		$(".selregion").change(function(){
		
			var region = $(this).val();
			
			$("input[type=checkbox][region='"+region+"']").prop("checked",$(this).is(":checked"));
			
		});
        $(".showteamdetails").click(function(event) {
			var expander = $(this).children("img");
			var nemID = $(this).attr("arg1");
			var victID = $(this).attr("arg2");
			var months = $(this).attr("arg3");
            if(expander.attr("src") == "img/minus.png")
            {
                expander.attr("src","img/plus.png");
            }
            else
            {
            // collapse all popupts
				$(".popup").hide();
                expander.attr("src","img/minus.png");
            }
		 
			var theDiv = $(this).next();
			var tPosX = event.pageX;
			var tPosY = event.pageY+10;
			theDiv.css({top: tPosY, left: tPosX});
			theDiv.toggle();
			//alert("nemesisdrilldown.php?nem="+nemID+"&vict="+victID+"&months="+months);
			theDiv.load("nemesisdrilldown.php?nem="+nemID+"&vict="+victID+"&months="+months);
			return false;
			});
		$("#pointsdetail").click(function(event) {
			
		 
			var theDiv = $(this).next();
			var tPosX = event.pageX-300;
			var tPosY = event.pageY+10;
			theDiv.css({top: tPosY, left: tPosX});
			theDiv.toggle();
			var racerID = $(this).attr("racerID");
			var AsOfDate = escape($(this).attr("AsOfDate"));
			theDiv.load("pointsdetail.php?racerID="+racerID+"&AsOfDate="+AsOfDate);
			return false;
			});
		$(".durationradio").click(function(event) {
				if($(this).val() == 'alltime')
				{
					$(".yearstat").hide();
					$(".careerstat").show();
				}
				else
				{
					$(".yearstat").show();
					$(".careerstat").hide();
				}
			});
		$("#commonopponentheader").click(function(event) {
				var expander = $(this).children(".toggler");
				var otherexpander = $("#nemesesheader").children(".toggler");
				
				if(expander.attr("src") == "img/minus.png")
				{
					expander.attr("src","img/plus.png");
					otherexpander.attr("src","img/minus.png");
				}
				else
				{
					expander.attr("src","img/minus.png");
					otherexpander.attr("src","img/plus.png");
				}
				$("#commonopponents").toggle("slow");
				$("#nemeses").toggle("slow");
				return false;
			});
		$("#nemesesheader .toggler").click(function(event) {
				var expander = $(this);
				var otherexpander = $("#commonopponentheader").children("");
				if(expander.attr("src") == "img/minus.png")
				{
					expander.attr("src","img/plus.png");
					otherexpander.attr("src","img/minus.png");
				}
				else
				{
					expander.attr("src","img/minus.png");
					otherexpander.attr("src","img/plus.png");
				}
				$("#commonopponents").toggle("slow");
				$("#nemeses").toggle("slow");
				return false;
			});
    });
	
    function showImages()
    {
        $("#frequencyfinish").attr("src",$("#frequencyfinish").attr("altsrc"));
        $("#frequencyfinish2").attr("src",$("#frequencyfinish2").attr("altsrc"));
        $("#frequencyfinish3").attr("src",$("#frequencyfinish3").attr("altsrc"));
    }
	var savedInterval = '1y';
    function ChangeGraph(interval)
    {
		var selected = $("#graphchanger").val();
		if(interval != '')
			savedInterval = interval;
		if(!savedInterval)
			savedInterval = '1y';
		
		var titles = new Array('% Beat','Points List Rank','Points Scored','% Beat Histogram');
		var urls= new Array('racerhistorygraph.php?racerID=15961&type=pct','racerhistorygraph.php?racerID=15961&type=ptslist&subtype=ptslist','racerhistorygraph.php?racerID=15961&type=pct&subtype=pts','racerhistorygraph.php?racerID=15961');
		var intervalText = "All Time";
		switch(savedInterval)
		{
			case '1m': intervalText = "Last Month"; break;
			case '3m': intervalText = "Last 3 Months"; break;
			case '1y': intervalText = "Last Year"; break;
			case '3y': intervalText = "Last 3 Years"; break;
		}
		$('#graphtarget').html('<img src=\"img/snake_transparent.gif\"/>');
		//$('#graphtarget').html("/" + urls[selected]+"&json=1&interval="+savedInterval);
		GraphDataService("/" + urls[selected]+"&json=1&interval="+savedInterval,updateChart);
		
		$('#graphtitle').html(titles[selected]+ " - "+intervalText);
		
		/*for(var i = 0; i < 4; i++)
		{
			if(graphs[i]== selected)
			{
				$("#"+graphs[i]).show();
				var url = urls[i] + "&interval="+savedInterval;
				alert(url);
				$("#"+graphs[i]+"img").attr('src',url);
			}
			else
				$("#"+graphs[i]).hide();
		}*/
		return false;
    }
	
</script>

As with any other metadata on this site, this information should be used as

	var map = new mapboxgl.Map({
		container: 'myMap',
		style: 'https://tilecdn.pinkbike.org/styles/trailforks-imperial/style.json',
		center: [-11.84664, 40.783726],
		zoom: 4
	  });


	var map;
    var lat;
	var lon;
	var geocoder = null;	
	var racesOnMap = new Array(); 
	
	function mapsLoaded() {	
         if(document.getElementById("myMap")) {
          var uluru = {lat: -25.363, lng: 131.044};
                var mapOptions = {
                    zoomControl: true,
                    zoomControlOptions: {
                        style: google.maps.ZoomControlStyle.SMALL
                        },
                   
                    mapTypeControl: false,
                    streetViewControl: false,
                    zoom: 9,
                    center: uluru,
                    mapTypeId: google.maps.MapTypeId.ROADMAP
                };
            map = new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById("myMap"), mapOptions);
       }

    function PlaceMarker(map, marker,latLng, centerMap,color,caption) {
        if (marker != null) {
            marker.setMap(null);
        }
        if(centerMap)
            map.setCenter(latLng);
        marker = new google.maps.Marker({
            map: map,
            position: latLng,
            title: caption//,

            //icon: '/Images/orange.png'
        });
        if (caption)
            marker.setTitle(caption);
        if (color)
            marker.setIcon("http://maps.google.com/mapfiles/ms/icons/"+color+"-dot.png")
        return marker;
    }

	function AddMarker(race)
	{
		//var latLong = new Microsoft.Maps.Location(race.RaceLat, race.RaceLon);
        var latlong = {lat: race.RaceLat,lng:race.RaceLon};
		
       
		
		
		var today = new Date();
		today.setFullYear(today.getFullYear()-1);
		
		if(race.RaceDate > today)
			var src='/img/wheelicon2.png';
		else
			var src='/img/wheelicon3.png';
		
	 var marker = new google.maps.Marker({
          position: latlong,
          map: map,
          title: race.RaceName,
          icon: src
        });
	}
